The Little Entente 72

Consults on the Current European Situation 73

Decision to Take Concerted Action ▲ National News Agency, Belgrade, 15th: The regular meeting of the foreign affairs authorities of Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Romania, the three Little Entente countries, held every six months, closed today. According to a statement issued tonight, the foreign affairs authorities of the three countries thoroughly discussed the current European situation and decided to take concerted action in future negotiations to restore the economic and political balance of Europe. Subsequently, the Czech Foreign Minister Benes told representatives of the press that the result of this meeting was that the three countries had fully agreed on all important issues. The current situation in Europe is extremely critical, but he, as an optimist, still believes that there is no despair and that it can be salvaged. Referring to the Lausanne Conference, he said that the three countries intend to adopt a moderate policy and not make concessions on any key points. The foreign affairs authorities of the three countries not only know that their interests are consistent but also believe that their interests are closely related to those of neighboring countries. The resolution of the problems in Central Europe cannot be achieved by the small countries alone and must rely on the goodwill and cooperation of other countries. U.S. House of Representatives

Report on Silver Issues 74

Advocates that the United States convene an international conference to find ways to restore the balance of gold and silver parity. ▲ National News Agency, Washington, 15th: The U.S. House of Representatives' Somers Silver Subcommittee has drafted a report in which a majority of the members agree that the U.S. President should invite countries that emphasize restoring prices to hold an international conference to stabilize finance and restore the balance of gold and silver parity through currency and other methods, thereby restoring prices. The report elaborates on the uneven distribution of gold and the inability of non-gold standard countries to repay debts. It believes that China will not necessarily be able to switch to the gold standard within two or three decades because its people are constrained by customs and are not yet prepared to adopt the gold standard credit standard. It also traces the causes of the world financial panic to the U.S. sale of silver in 1929 and 1920, India's switch to the gold standard, and the destruction of silver coins in 1928 and 1929, which led to international exchange chaos. It also states that after the fall in silver prices in Asia, capital in silver units became gold units. With the disuse of gold, there was a growing shortage, and the central banks of gold standard countries felt their gold reserves were dwindling daily. Therefore, when China continues to use the silver standard, the parity of gold and silver must be balanced to avoid excessive disparity. If an international conference can reverse the current gold reserve method, the Far East does not need to store gold for exchange purposes, and gold worth US$100 billion can be released for other uses.

Lindbergh Investigates Kidnappers 75

▲ Reuters, Hopewell, 16th: Lindbergh's son's ashes will be buried next to his grandfather Morrow's grave. Morrow passed away last year when Mr. and Mrs. Lindbergh were in China. Colonel Lindbergh is now leading guards carrying automatic rifles, hoping to find maritime bandits, fearing that the bandits may want to kidnap Colonel Lindbergh in order to escape the law. The bandits who previously demanded a ransom of 50,000 yuan from Colonel Lindbergh now tell shipbuilding tycoon Ketches that they were also deceived and that the ransom has been transferred to others, but they have obtained the person's whereabouts. It is now known that there were formerly ten gangs of bandits who planned to use this kidnapping case to extort money from Colonel Lindbergh.

Foreign News Two

Shipping Magnate Dollar Passes Away 76

▲ Reuters, San Rafael, California, 16th: Robert Dollar, the old owner of the Dollar Shipping Company, passed away today at the age of eighty-eight. Dollar worked hard throughout his life. Not long ago, he still traveled to the East. After returning to the country, he was bedridden for some time before recovering. Unexpectedly, he fell ill again this time and passed away. Dollar was born in Falkirk, Scotland. He first entered elementary school and left school at the age of eleven. He then went to Canada, and at the age of thirteen, he worked as a hired hand on a timber farm. Later he came to the United States, and it was not until April 1888, at the age of forty-four, that he became a U.S. citizen. He lived in San Francisco and made a profit from foreign trade and the lumber industry, eventually becoming one of the world's great shipping magnates. Years ago, he changed Dollar Shipping to the World Line, and the business flourished. Later, he built two of the largest American merchant ships, the President Hoover and the President Coolidge. Dollar was a great traveler and continued to travel even in his later years. At the age of eighty, he still took air tours. After many years away from his hometown, Dollar once returned to visit. His comrades in Scotland presented him with the freedom of the city of Falkirk. Dollar was also a freeman of New York and Boston.

French Merchant Ship "Georges Philippar" Encounters Disaster 77

▲ Reuters, Athens, 16th: The French company's new large merchant ship Georges Philippar, carrying 600 passengers from the Far East, suddenly encountered disaster a few miles from Cape Gata Fui. It has now been abandoned. It is reported that several passengers were seriously injured in the fire. It is not yet known if there were any fatalities. At 5:45 this morning (local time), the ship sent out a distress signal, and all nearby ships rushed to the rescue, including the Soviet merchant ship "Kenifort," the British merchant ship "Masout," the British Steamship Company's "Kaisereihint," the Eastern Company's "Waterland," and a Japanese merchant ship. The first three ships to arrive used lifeboats and rafts to rescue many passengers. At that time, the captain of the wrecked ship had decided to abandon the ship. The Japanese ship saw an empty lifeboat en route. It is not known whether the people in the boat were killed. Later, we received a telegram stating that the merchant ship "Kontrelektor" rescued 129 people and the "Masout" rescued 134 people and sailed to Athens. The captain of the wrecked ship was also rescued and is on the Soviet merchant ship. That merchant ship and the remaining ships rescued many people, but the details have not yet been received. Another telegram stated that two sailors escaped onto a raft and are feared to have drifted away. (It is reported that the wrecked French ship sailed from Shanghai to Europe on April 23.)

Earthquake in the Dutch East Indies 78

▲ Reuters, Batavia, 15th: There was an earthquake in the Menado area of Celebes Island in the Dutch East Indies today, lasting one minute. Residents were terrified. There was considerable damage, with five people killed, twenty seriously injured, and more than one hundred and fifty houses collapsed. Important news.

League of Nations on the First Report

Fear That Disputes Will Arise 79

▲ Opinion of the New Chairman of the Council, Madariaga ▲ If Japan Has Objections, Consult The Hague Judicial Tribunal ▲ Nagoya Shimbun says that the League of Nations Council has different interpretations of the interim report of the investigation committee chairman, Lytton, and Japan, and it is feared that disputes will be unavoidable in the future of the meeting. That is, Japan absolutely does not allow the League of Nations to interfere in the Manchuria issue and opposes the League of Nations citing Article 15 of the Covenant, while the Council will transfer Lytton's interim report to the General Assembly for resolution. However, regarding the relationship between the powers of the General Assembly and the Council, there are differences of opinion within the League of Nations. Secretary-General Drummond has communicated his own interpretation in the form of a memorandum to all parties. The content is quite unfavorable to Japan. Therefore, Japanese representative Nagaoka is striving for the League of Nations to carefully consider and implement Japan's claims. ▲ Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun says that the new chairman of the League of Nations Council, Madariaga, transferred the first report of the League of Nations investigation team to the General Assembly for discussion. If Japan raises objections, the Council will consult the International Court of Justice in The Hague for its ruling. The League of Nations believes that this procedure is legal in view of the internal atmosphere of the Hague Court. However, it is generally observed that the investigation team's report has no substantial significance, and Japan will certainly not take any actions that will cause more disputes. United States Coastal Defense

Change Equipment Plan 80

Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun says that the United States Navy Department has decided to change its equipment plan for U.S. coastal defense. That is, the previous plan to equip battleships with 14-inch to 16-inch guns for attack is being changed. Due to the recent changes in the ship types of the navies of various countries, the United States will equip mostly light cruisers with 8-inch guns, reduce large-caliber weapons, and equip automatic long-range guns to fortify fortresses.

Inspection Record of Shanhaiguan 81

▲The Course of Japanese Provocation ▲Conversation with Brigade Commander He

A dispatch from Beiping: Since the 7th, Japanese troops have been firing cannons and guns day and night in Shanhaiguan, which has effectively become a very serious situation, as Shanhaiguan is the gateway to Pingjin. Since the signing of the agreement in Shanghai, the Japanese have wanted to shift their forces to the Northeast, so they intend to occupy Shanhaiguan. Regarding this tense situation and its progression, our reporter went to investigate and records the details as follows. The reporter departed from Ping on the BeiNing Railway train at 8:00 p.m. on the 10th. Upon arriving in Tianjin, more than ten Japanese soldiers boarded the train, including four in plainclothes. The armed Japanese soldiers searched the entire train, as if looking for something, causing unease among all the passengers. The next morning at 7:00 a.m., the train arrived in Qinhuangdao. The Japanese flag flew over the south platform, and armed Japanese soldiers showed their fierce faces, staring at the passengers. It is said that four Japanese warships did arrive at the Qinhuangdao seaside pier the day before yesterday, including one aircraft carrier. Its 300 marines landed the day before yesterday and went to Shanhaiguan on foot. Last night, they returned from Shanhaiguan, some stationed on the warship and some in the barracks. Unfortunately, the train only stopped for about ten minutes in Qinhuangdao, so it was not possible to investigate the local situation. Before the train departed, more Japanese soldiers boarded and followed the train to Shanhaiguan. At 8:10 a.m., the train arrived at Shanhaiguan Station. The reporter got off the train to inspect the situation at the station. As soon as I arrived at the station building, I saw the large sign of the pseudo Fengshan Railway station building hanging on the wall. Kan Duo, the head of the pseudo railway bureau, posted a notice with the date "April 12, Datong Year 1" at the end. Looking at the uniforms of the police in the station, although they were no different from (BeiNing), the cap badges had been replaced with pseudo national emblems. Our country's BeiNing Railway station building is in the west. Passengers who want to take the train to buy tickets must ask someone for directions. After passing the overpass, I saw a white cloth banner of more than ten feet hanging next to the waiting room, which read "(Manchukuo Border Surveillance Police Team Branch)." There were policemen dressed as armed Japanese soldiers in the station, with two people stationed at each post, wearing a golden bell on their hats, black riding boots, and holding new-style rifles. Listening to their accents, most of them were Japanese, but there were also a dozen or so Chinese. The pseudo-national police came from Jinzhou and forcibly occupied the BeiNing Railway station building. After negotiations by the general section chief Kou Bin, the pseudo-national police moved to the middle platform. In short, the order of the station is very chaotic, because there are three types of police in the station. In fact, the pseudo Fengshan Railway occupies more than one-third of the station building. Our service personnel are in a state of tyrannical and unreasonable behavior, and can only swallow their anger. The police sent by the pseudo-country are not limited to the station, and sometimes go to the South Gate, so there are many Japanese residents in the section from the station to the South Gate, and there are two hotels, Yamato and Daito, which specialize in accommodating Japanese, Koreans, and Chinese traitors. In the South Gate, there is a Japanese military police team, with barbed wire covering the four walls. Inside the gate are piles of sacks about ten feet high, with machine guns mounted on them. Many Japanese in plain clothes enter and exit, and their actions are suspicious. Japanese soldiers carry pistols and travel in groups of three or five in the streets. When they see Chinese soldiers, they glare at them. There are four soldiers of the Ninth Brigade guarding the South Gate of Shanhaiguan, dressed neatly. He Zhuguo, the commander of the Ninth Brigade, lives in front of the Education Bureau in the city. On the screen wall of the brigade headquarters are four large characters "(Mountains and Rivers Confront)," written by He himself. Each city gate in the city has soldiers of the Ninth Brigade guarding it, and the situation is no different from the past. The local security of Shanhaiguan is the responsibility of He Zhuguo, County Magistrate Li Shufan, and Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Baozhen. The cause of this outrageous action by the Japanese army was Matsushita, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Yushu. Last month, he heard that Brigade Commander He's subordinates had captured a thief. Matsushita said that the thief was a volunteer army and demanded that he be extradited for Japanese punishment. At that time, He Zhuguo happened to be in Beiping. The Japanese forced the extradition, interrogated him, and released him. At the same time, Matsushita used the excuse of the Boxer Protocol to claim that if railways, electric wires, and buildings were damaged within two English miles of the BeiNing Line near Shanhaiguan and Luanxian, the troops stationed in each country could arrest them. Therefore, he wanted to use this to stop the activities of the volunteer army. On the afternoon of the 3rd of this month, at 4:00 p.m., he took a prepared agreement to the brigade headquarters to see Brigade Commander He, limiting He to sign it immediately. The content stated that the Japanese army and navy had the right to directly arrest and detain in order to prevent the volunteer army from operating in Chinese territory, and made considerable explanations regarding the garrison from Shanhaiguan to Luanzhou. Brigade Commander He saw that this matter was important and sternly refused. Because He refused to sign, Matsushita went to the county government with Staff Officer Miura to see County Magistrate Li Shufan and made the same request. County Magistrate Li also refused, and Matsushita returned angrily. On the 5th, the pseudo Fengshan Railway train suddenly transported more than 200 people from Jinzhou, Korea, and lived in Yamato and Daito, so rumors spread in Yuguan. At 11:00 p.m. on the 7th, a Japanese armored train with more than 80 Japanese soldiers and police officers arrived at a location four or five miles away from Shanhaiguan and suddenly fired live ammunition with pistols for about half an hour, causing great panic among the residents of the city. Brigade Commander He went to the southeast corner of the city to inspect the situation. Before long, the Japanese armored train drove away. The next morning, Brigade Commander He sent someone to question the Japanese side. The Japanese side said it was a night drill. At 4:00 p.m. on the 8th, 70 Japanese police officers threw hand grenades in the southeast of Shanhaiguan City, and there was a constant booming sound. From 8:00 a.m. to 10:00 a.m. on the 9th, the Japanese army fired live ammunition outside Dongguan again. At 9:30 a.m., they switched to machine guns. At that time, all the people in the city heard the sound of machine guns. At 11:00 p.m. that night, Hirata, the captain of the Japanese military police team outside the South Gate, led his subordinates to fire guns in the barracks, also using live ammunition. Immediately, several Japanese military police officers suddenly rushed out of the barracks with small pistols and rushed to the outside of the South Gate. One of the Japanese military police officers spoke Chinese and wanted to see Brigade Commander He, saying that there was an urgent matter to discuss. Our guarding soldiers were ordered to remain calm, so the Japanese military police rushed to the city without firing a shot, fortunately not causing any incidents. On the 10th, the Japanese military and police were slightly silent, so there was no shelling or shooting. Also, on the 9th, Japanese soldiers appeared in the Lijiabao Mayingzi area outside Jiukoukou and threw hand grenades. Seeing that the disruption plan was unsuccessful, the Japanese asked Brigade Commander He Zhuguo to give up Jiukoukou in Shanhaiguan and let the Japanese army garrison it. At the same time, Japanese troops were stationed near Shimenzhai in Jiukoukou. He politely refused. Early on the 11th, a Japanese train with about 400 soldiers arrived at the former station. After getting off the train, they advanced towards Jiukoukou. The actions have not yet received an accurate report. The Japanese barracks south of the railway have been building trenches and repairing fortresses for days, with barbed wire nets installed around the barracks. There are short cannons in the trenches, with the gun jackets removed, and the muzzles facing the South Gate of Shanhaiguan. The Japanese military strength in Shanhaiguan is about 400 to 500 people. It is found that if our side has to implement self-defense in response to this provocative action by Japan, the entire city will be devastated. The local authorities have also studied countermeasures and formed a special police team with police in the city to maintain the security of the South Gate, because the area is close to the Japanese army and is most prone to misunderstandings. This special police force has been on duty the day before yesterday. He Zhuguo and Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Shishen ordered special protection for Japanese residents to prevent the Japanese from having any excuses. However, the Kwantung Army Headquarters in Shenyang and the Tianjin Japanese Garrison Army Headquarters have sent Japanese military officers to Yuguan secretly for several days. Their actions are very noteworthy. It is said that the purpose of the Japanese side is to make every effort to quell the north of Manchuria, but in order to consolidate the gateway to the rear, Shanhaiguan is essential. If it cannot be occupied, there is a risk that the rear will be constrained. Therefore, the situation in Shanhaiguan is getting tighter every day. After the reporter entered the city, he visited He Zhuguo at his private residence and asked about the situation of defending the territory and his personal aspirations for the future. He said the following: "(Since the September 18th Incident, Shanhaiguan has been in an unusually important position. Matsushita, the captain of the Japanese garrison, previously made unreasonable demands to prevent the activities of the volunteer army, forcing me to sign and intimidating me with harsh words. As a soldier, I only know how to defend the territory, so I refused immediately. The Japanese army then used the trick of using exercises to disturb the local area. I negotiated to stop it on the one hand, and on the other hand, I gave special protection to Japanese residents. Our troops are stationed in the city, and the soldiers guarding the gate are responsible for training with experience. There are about 80 pseudo-national police officers who have arrived in Shanhaiguan. They stated in advance that they were here to maintain the order of the Fengshan Road. Now they have gone beyond the scope, and I have negotiated with the Japanese side based on reason. As for the future, I only know that I have a country and do not consider anything else. Regarding the Japanese army firing guns, because it affects local security, I am negotiating with the Japanese side, and it may be resolved." He has very strict requirements for his subordinates, so he has a very good relationship with the local people. After the reporter said goodbye, he went inside and outside the city to investigate the social situation. It is reported that merchants are leaving because the Japanese army is causing trouble, but business is as usual. South Gate Street is more lively, and most of the shoppers are railway workers. Most of the shops are restaurants, and they usually sell pot stickers. There are vendors selling prawns everywhere, and you can buy six or seven for each corner. According to the shrimp vendors, the prawns are all shipped from Andong Yingkou, and the value is very cheap, so people who buy prawns are also enthusiastic. South Gate Street is slightly inferior to South Gate in terms of commerce, with more transactions in rice and grain. The county government is inside the South Gate, and the houses are dilapidated. The East Gate is (The First Pass Under Heaven). Under the pass is the Tian Family Elementary School, which is slightly larger in scale and run by Tanaka Gyoku. Looking from the city tower, you can see Mount Jue opposite, 30 miles away from the pass, towering into the clouds. Inside the First Pass Under Heaven tower, there is still a large area of square, and the characters are more majestic than those hanging outside. It is said that the one in the house is the true pen, and the outside is Yingding. Following the city road south, Qiufeng Pavilion is next to the city. At the battlements of the city, there are four or five guards. From the city, you can see the pseudo-Manchu flag next to the railway. After getting off the city tower, I went to the Education Bureau. The rural normal school and county middle school run by the bureau are located in the bureau, with a total of four or five hundred students, of which more than one hundred are normal school students, all wearing light brown uniforms, and are energetic. During the Japanese army's artillery exercises, classes were held as usual. Shanhaiguan Station has a Rotary School, and the students are all children of railway employees. Recently, the school authorities have planned to move the school into the city because the order in the station is very chaotic. Because of the current situation, very few students go to school. Anti-Japanese Martyrs 82

▲Organizing a Burial Committee

In this Battle of Songhu, which lasted for months, loyal and brave soldiers sacrificed their lives for the country. Without proper commendation, it would not be enough to comfort the loyal souls and heroic spirits. The Central Party Department and the Military Commission, in view of this, specially gathered various party, military, and political organs and related troops to organize the Songhu Anti-Japanese Martyrs Burial Committee in order to investigate surnames, collect remains, build tombs and engrave stones, and make them immortal. The articles of association of the association are copied as follows. Articles of Association of the Songhu Anti-Japanese Martyrs Burial Committee: (1) In order to prepare for the burial of the martyrs who died in the anti-Japanese operations in Songhu area to commend their loyalty, the Songhu Anti-Japanese Martyrs Burial Committee is specially established to handle it. (2) This committee is organized by representatives of the following agencies: one representative from the Central Party Department, one representative from the Military Commission, one representative from the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs, one representative from the Military Medical Department, one representative from the 19th Route Army (including the 6th Regiment of the Military Police), one representative from the 60th Division, one representative from the 61st Division, one representative from the 78th Division, one representative from the 5th Army, one representative from the 87th Division, one representative from the 88th Division, one representative from the Wusong Fortress, one representative from the Tax Police Brigade, two representatives from the Martyrs Cemetery Preparatory Office, Comrade Fu Huan Guang of the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum. (3) The Central Party Department representative shall be the chairman of this committee. (4) The main tasks to be handled by the committee are: 1. Investigation and registration of martyrs, 2. Search for the remains of martyrs, 3. Relocation and burial, 4. Construction of cemeteries, 5. Establishment of memorial halls and monuments, 6. Memorial services and sacrifices. (5) The committee shall be under the guidance of the Military Commission, and the progress of various matters such as funding, transportation, and burial shall be negotiated by the Martyrs Cemetery Preparatory Committee and the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs. (6) The business divisions and rules of procedure of the committee shall be drafted by the committee and submitted for approval and implementation. Guangdong troops aid Fujian

Focusing on the Fujian-Jiangxi Border 83

▲Red bandits Attempt to Disturb Guangdong's Pingyuan Territory ▲Guangdong Side Uncovers Reddening Three Provinces Plan

A dispatch from Shantou: The main force of the Fujian southern communist bandits has recently moved south from Changting to the area between Longyan and Nanjing, with a tendency to move to the Jiangxi border of Xunwu and overlook Pingyuan. Therefore, after the Guangdong army recovered Yongding and Shanghang, it also focused on the Jiangxi border, and it was not convenient to go deep into western Fujian. Yesterday, the Shantou Third Army Office received a telegram from Huang Zhiwen, the commander of the Pingyuan Eighth Division, stating that the bandits who attacked the Fen Shuiqiu camp yesterday (the 10th) were the entire 36th Division of the Pseudo 12th Army (Deng Zihui) and the Red Guard local communists, totaling about 3,000 people, with machine guns and repeating cannons. After I dispatched Chen Tuanfu and Peng Ying to assist, the bandits were completely repelled at 2:00 p.m. More than 60 bandits were killed, more than 100 were injured, one bandit was captured, and four rifles were seized. According to the captured prisoner, the Red bandits who went to Xunwu on the 2nd included the entire 36th Division of the Pseudo 12th Army, totaling 106, 107, and 108 three battalions, and the First and Second Independent Divisions. Each battalion of the 36th Division has three infantry companies and one machine gun company, with more than 80 people in each company and more than 70 guns, with 150 rounds of ammunition for each gun. The bandit transfer to Xunwu has the intention of invading Pingyuan to disturb the rear of our army entering Fujian. Currently, the entire Qiu Ying company is stationed in Fen Shuiqiu, and one company each of Peng Ying and Zhang Ying, and the rest are stationed in Bao Cheng. Today (the 11th), the bandits will attack again, and the number of people will increase compared to yesterday. The rest will be reported later, etc. Also, Huang Zhiwen's telegram on the 8th stated that he had just received a telephone report from Regiment Commander Ye Shouyao, stating that the bandits who attacked Fen Shuiqiu last night had been in contact from 10:30 p.m. to 4:30 a.m. this morning, and then retreated to Xunwu County on the Jiangxi border. It was found that the number of bandits who attacked this time was only more than 200, and the purpose was actually to harass. As a result, our side injured one squad leader, captured one bandit, and seized one gun, etc. According to the above observations, the Guangdong army entering Fujian has already been in contact with the bandits on the Jiangxi border. The bandits on the side of the Jiangxi border will not be cleared without going deep into the Fujian border. The Chao and Shantou areas are still defended by the Independent Second Division Zhang Ruigui's troops. Zhang and the division's special service battalion arrived in Shantou on the 8th. According to Zhang's interview with the reporter, although the division headquarters moved to Shantou, a part of the officials still stayed in Chaoyang to handle the aftermath of Nanshan. When the division first entered Nanshan, it found small groups of communist bandits. Once they were suppressed, they would disperse and disappear, suspected of fleeing elsewhere. Unexpectedly, the bandits were cunning and hid deep in the mountains. The officers and soldiers were unfamiliar with the place and were often attacked. Later, they changed their plan, surrounded the entire mountain, cut off their food supply, and blocked their news transmission. Every day, they sent sentries and spies to scout around. As soon as they saw the bandits, they would send teams to suppress them. In the past two months, there have been hundreds of battles, large and small. All the large groups of communist bandits have been scattered and eliminated by seven or eight out of ten. The organ of the Pseudo Dongjiang Military Commission was seized in the mountains, and important documents and plans were found. The content was to prepare for an internal response from the Jiangxi bandits and set the uprising at the end of March (more than ten days after Zhang's division entered the suppression), and first capture Chaoyang, Puning, Huilai, Jieyang, Chaoan, Shantou, and Chenghai. All the organizations were quite sophisticated. That is, the communist bandits in Jiangxi Province invaded Zhangzhou and stationed troops in Changting, and there were also liaison operations. Fortunately, they took the initiative to attack and broke the bandit's nest, so that the bandits could not cause trouble (the 12th).

Zhengyang Plundered by Bandits 84

▲Central Government Sends Troops to Suppress ▲Rumor Says Bandits Have Fled to Bengbu

A dispatch from Bengbu: After the bandits on the Anhui border captured Zhengyang, they plundered wantonly. Many firearms were confiscated from the local garrison and Tuan Police, and several merchants and civilians were killed. When the bandits first entered the street, there were only a few hundred people, and the residents who fled were like a tide. Fortunately, Yu Yumen, the head of the town's security group, led the team to cover the retreat, saving many refugees. However, there were too many refugees, and they were in a panic to cross the river. Many people were squeezed into the water and drowned. Yu arrived in Bengbu yesterday, and his troops suffered slight losses. Niu Youchen, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, also escaped safely. Shou Zhen people in Bengbu, in view of the spread of the Red disaster and the suffering of their hometowns, have been telegraphing the central government for days to request troops to assist in the suppression. The Military Commission has ordered the First Division Hu Zongnan, the Fourth Division Xu Tingyao, and the Independent 33rd Brigade Tang Yunshan to rush to suppress the bandits. The advance station soldiers of the Fourth Division arrived in Bengbu yesterday, and most of the troops will continue to arrive from Pukou within days, and will go west along Huaihe. The First Division will go to Anqing and advance from Tongcheng Shucheng to Hefei, turning to Liuan to join the troops of Chen Tiaoyuan Wang Jun, etc. to suppress the bandits. The 33rd Brigade has already started from Henan and is rushing into Anhui. The Bengbu Office of the Independent 40th Brigade of the Army here received a wireless telegraph from Li Ruian, the chief of staff of the brigade, from Huoqiu last night, saying that the advance troops of the 718th Regiment of the brigade were in fierce battle with the Red bandits near Zhengyang. I personally led the 720th Regiment to advance and surround the Red bandits. Huoqiu was guarded by a part of the 718th Regiment, together with the county police preparation camp Sun Peiji's troops, etc. The bandits once approached Thirty Li Pu in Shouxian. Zhu Dexin, the chairman of the Shouxian Chamber of Commerce, telegraphed the Bengbu Chamber of Commerce again last night, begging for troops to assist. It is reported that the bandit suppression army has been in contact with the bandits near Shouxian, and the fighting is fierce. Ni Rongxian, the commander-in-chief of the militia, also ordered the troops from Fuyang to go to Zheng and attack the Red bandits. Ni arrived in Fengtai last night. According to a military agency receiving a telegram from Fengtai, the bandits in Zhengyang have already withdrawn, taking away many hostages when they left. The local losses were very heavy. According to refugees from Zheng to Bengbu, the bandits searched and plundered a lot of silver dollars, rice, and salt, and loaded them on boats, with the intention of taking them away. The copper coins and flour that were searched and plundered were distributed to the poor, etc. Approximately, the bandits saw that the armies and militias from all sides were attacking Zhengyang, and the number of people was small and it was difficult to resist, so they carried out a large-scale looting and left. As for Shouying

Page 8

Feng Huai and other counties, although they were tense a few days ago, are now all peaceful. The military and police authorities here have stepped up security these days. The city has been under martial law from 10:00 p.m. every night. Pedestrians are not allowed to pass without a password. The ground security responsibility is borne by the troops of Zeng Wanzhong of the 12th Division. Songjiang 85

▲Doctor Cheats and Rapes Female Teacher

A female teacher from a certain girls' school behind Puzhao Temple in the city is quite sociable and has been engaged to a certain Song. The two are deeply in love and visit frequently. Unable to restrain themselves, they secretly conceived. The woman, seeing her belly gradually growing, felt it was very inappropriate and sought ways to eliminate it. She met a Hakka western doctor, Wu, somewhere and discussed it with him. Unexpectedly, the doctor had been coveting her for a long time and readily agreed to take on the task. One night, he asked the woman to go for a diagnosis. When she arrived, he pretended that the hospital room was too small and led her to open room number five in a hotel. Under the pretext of diagnosing the uterus, he induced the woman to undress and lie on her back. The doctor then intimidated her to keep silent and carried out his rape. The woman's will was weak and she fell into his trap, feeling extremely frustrated. She returned to school in tears the next morning. This matter was gradually heard by her fiancé, who came to the school to investigate, and the drama of the female teacher being deceived and raped by a doctor was exposed. It is unknown how this case will end in the future.

Suzhou 86

▲Anti-Japanese Association Warns Treacherous Merchants

The Wuxian Anti-Japanese Association had been suspended indefinitely since the outbreak of the war. Now that the war has come to an end, it is still working hard. It was found that Lao Deji Pharmacy was privately selling Japanese goods "Riyue Water" in Yuyang Lane, which was resolved by the General Assembly to fine 100 yuan and publish the photo of the treacherous merchant in the newspaper to serve as a warning.

Wuxi 87

▲Party and Government Mediate Labor Dispute

The Qianshen Silk Factory on Tongyun Bridge caused a labor dispute due to the female workers' exams and talent selection, which caused a misunderstanding among the old ladies. Yesterday, the party and government gathered representatives of labor and capital to hold a meeting to mediate and resolved: (1) Regarding the recruitment of workers, both parties will go back and determine the most concessions, and then discuss again. (2) Regarding age, it is set as (A) Youth group, from 16 to 26 years old; (B) Middle-aged group, from 27 to 36 years old. Those with excellent work are not restricted by age. Regarding other aspects, they will be negotiated after the first article is resolved.

▲78th Division Shoots Deserters

Four soldiers of the first company of the fourth regiment of the 78th Division stationed in Xihui Mountain fled with their weapons the night before last. The next morning, they were inspected by the road-guarding military police at the Shitangwan Station. Because they resisted the accusation, one person was killed on the spot. A total of three people, including Liu Dezhu, Yuan Xiubao, and Li Shixiu, were captured and sent to the battalion headquarters. After being informed that the private escape was true, they were shot immediately to show a warning.

▲Murder Case Offender Sentenced to Imprisonment

Li Zupei, who opened the Liangxi Hotel on Tongyun Road, was stabbed to death with a bayonet by Jie Pifu Arong, colluding with wounded soldier Huang Weisheng, etc., in Doumen Qin Lane on the 7th of last month. The murderer was completely arrested by the garrisoned military police and sent to the Nanjing Military Police Headquarters after being informed. Now it has been found that Fu Arong and Huang Weisheng have each been sentenced to eight years of imprisonment. Accomplices Peng Boting, Hu Mingyun, Shao Haiquan, Chen Yuena, Lu Dexing, and Zhou De and six others were each sentenced to three months of imprisonment.

Jiangyin 88

▲Forgery of Documents Case Judgment

He Shipan, the general director of the Jiangyin Branch of the China Road Association, was sued by President Zhao Zongyi for a case of forgery of documents. After the county was informed, the judgment was pronounced on the afternoon of the 13th. He Shipan was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment and deprived of public rights for two years.

Zhenjiang 89

▲Resolution to Oppose the Unsealing of Enemy Goods

The Zhenjiang business community had approximately 500,000 yuan worth of goods sealed up during the previous crackdown on Japanese goods. Since the outbreak of the Songhu War, social and economic panic has occurred, and various industries have requested the party and government authorities of this province to allow the unsealing and sale to provide financial relief to the provincial capital. The Provincial Party Department ordered the Provincial Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to discuss it carefully. The association convened a meeting of all sectors yesterday, with more than 20 people attending. It was resolved to oppose the unsealing of Japanese goods and issued a declaration, which was drafted by the student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association.

Nantong 90

▲Langshan Fortress to Build Forts

The General Staff Headquarters of the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs, with Langshan in Nantong as a natural danger in the Yangtze River, specially sent Zhu Wei, Gong Jizhi, Gao Yunqu, and the German Flemai Li to Tong on the 15th to survey the terrain of the fortress. It is reported that the result of the survey determined Junshan in the southeast of Langshan to build a fort, because the mountain is appropriately located at the Lang Fu ferry at Baimao Sand estuary, which is extremely dangerous. A plan will be drawn up and submitted to the ministry for approval.

Gao You 91

▲ Dispute over the construction of a dike in Bao Ying. The Dawei in southern Bao Ying is of great importance to the farmland irrigation of Gao and Bao counties. This time, Gao and Bao counties will jointly repair it, and Yan Zuobin of Bao Ying is appointed as the chief director, and Jin Zhaoqu of Gao You is the deputy director. Previously, Yan requested the Gao You Relief Bureau to allocate relief flour but was not approved. Yan then changed the route and built the dike to the east to defend the Dawei, and forced farmers in Gao You territory to demolish houses and give up land, and forcibly destroyed rice seedling beds. Liu Tianguan and other affected farmers in the tenth district of this county came to the city to appeal to the party and government organs. The county government dispatched Wang Qilin to investigate together with He Zhuoru of the Party Department and immediately stopped the digging of the fields. Unexpectedly, Yan and others not only refused to obey, but also arrested the farmers' representatives Shen Furong, Zhu Shufang, Chen Shoupeng, and Liu Tianfu, who have not been released yet. It is now reported that 58 affected farmers including Liu Tianguan have telegraphed the provincial government for legal action.

Rugao 92

▲ Three men and women killed by bandits. In an open space about a mile south of Dongyan Village, Lugang District, Rugao, Miao Ya Ru and his wife from Jiang'an, who were addicted to opium, and Liu Jingsheng were passing by when several bandits suddenly came towards them with box guns. Without asking any questions, they shot and killed the three of them, leaving their bodies by the roadside and leaving. Education News

Temporary Regulations for the Organization of Education Bureaus in Various Counties 105

| and Standards for Expenditure | The Education Department of Jiangsu Province, under orders, believes that in this time of national crisis, all expenses should be reduced as much as possible so that we can overcome difficulties together. Therefore, it has revised the organizational regulations of the education bureaus of various counties, as well as the classification standards and expenditure table, and submitted them to the Ministry of Education for review and record. It is found that the expenditures of provincial schools and social education institutions under the jurisdiction of this department have always been paid from the provincial education expenditure. How the budget should be reduced should be discussed and implemented by the Education Expenditure Committee. The education bureaus of the remaining counties are responsible for managing the educational administration of the entire county. Although their nature belongs to administration, their internal organization and external measures are very different from those of other county bureaus. Therefore, although austerity is an important goal, the methods of austerity cannot be the same as those of other county bureaus. Moreover, education is an important foundation for the country, and it should be vigorously expanded to achieve universal coverage. We must not give up eating for fear of choking, causing criticism of being stuck in the mud. Moreover, the education funds of various counties mostly have special funds, and the independence of education funds has been repeatedly ordered in recent years, which is very different from other administrative expenses that affect the provincial treasury. Therefore, the way to reduce expenses should start with saving administrative expenses. All redundant personnel and wasteful expenses that do not contribute to practical work should be strictly eliminated. Other expenses that are indeed used for business purposes should remain as they are, so as not to hinder future development. With this method, the intention of attaching importance to education can still be implied in the act of complying with official orders. This department has revised the original organizational regulations of the education bureaus of various counties in this province based on this purpose, and revised the classification standards and expenditure table for the expenses that should be paid by the education bureaus of various counties, referring to the actual situation, so as to follow. As for the education bureaus of various counties, except for Gaoyou and other four counties that have been changed to education sections due to flood disasters, the remaining ones are planned to continue to set up bureaus to take special responsibility. The said regulations and standards have been approved by the 489th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee. In addition to the case, the reasons for the austerity method, along with a copy of the draft regulations and the classification standards and expenditure table, are submitted with the text, hoping to be reviewed and filed for record. After receiving the submission, the Ministry of Education yesterday consulted the Jiangsu Provincial Government to instruct the Education Department, saying that the standard original regulations, etc., are generally not inappropriate and can be filed for record. However, the words (temporary) should be added above the words regulations in the original title, and the words (to be selected by the bureau director and submitted to the county government for transfer to the education department for approval and appointment) should be added above Article 6 and Article 7 (whose regulations are to be determined separately).

(1) Revised Temporary Regulations for the Organization of Education Bureaus in Various Counties in Jiangsu Province 106

Article 1: The county education bureau shall be composed of the director of the education bureau, county supervisors, education committee members, and a number of bureau staff. Article 2: The county education bureau shall be divided into five levels according to the amount of county education funds. The classification standards and expenditure table shall be determined separately. Article 3: The county education bureau shall be responsible for school education, social education, and other cultural undertakings in the entire county. Article 4: The director of the county education bureau shall be under the command of the director of the education department and the county magistrate, supervise and manage the affairs of the bureau, and command and supervise the education institutions under its jurisdiction. Article 5: The director of the county education bureau shall be selected by the county magistrate from two or three persons who have noble character, embrace the party principles, and meet one of the following qualifications, and shall be submitted to the education department for submission to the provincial government for approval and appointment. When necessary, the education department may directly submit to the provincial government for appointment. (1) Those who have passed the teaching examination of the former university district or have been qualified by the provincial government's identification. (2) Graduates of domestic and foreign university education colleges, normal universities, or advanced normal specialized courses who have held educational positions for more than one year. (3) Graduates of the former provincial normal specialized course who have held educational positions for more than two years. (4) Graduates of the normal school undergraduate course or high school normal course who have held educational positions for more than three years. (5) Graduates of specialized schools or above who have held educational positions for more than three years and have achieved certain results. Article 6: The county supervisor shall, under the command of the director of the education bureau, inspect and guide educational matters in the entire county, and shall be selected by the bureau director and submitted to the county government for transfer to the education department for approval and appointment. The regulations shall be determined separately. Article 7: The county education bureau shall divide the entire county into several school districts, and submit them to the county government for transfer to the education department for approval. Each school district shall have one education committee member, who shall, under the command of the bureau director, command, supervise, and handle educational affairs in the entire district, and shall be selected by the bureau director and submitted to the county government for transfer to the education department for approval and appointment. The regulations shall be determined separately. Article 8: The staff members of the county education bureau shall be selected by the bureau director and submitted to the county government for approval and appointment for filing with the education department. Article 9: The county education bureau may appoint employees as needed. Article 10: The expenses of the county education bureau shall be paid from the county education funds. Article 11: The detailed rules for handling affairs of the county education bureau shall be formulated by the education bureau and submitted to the county government for transfer to the education department for approval and implementation. Article 12: The county education bureau shall establish an education administrative committee and an economic audit committee. The rules shall be determined separately. Article 13: These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented after being resolved by the Provincial Government Committee, and shall be reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

(2) Classification Standards and Expenditure Table for Education Bureaus in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province 107

Level 1: County education funds of 400,000 yuan or more, annual administrative expenses of 16,320 yuan, annual salary of the bureau director of 1,440 yuan, annual salary of the county supervisor of 960 yuan. (Level 2) County education funds of 300,000 yuan or more, annual administrative expenses of 13,740 yuan, annual salary of the bureau director of 1,440 yuan, annual salary of the supervisor of 840 yuan. (Level 3) County education funds of 200,000 yuan or more, annual administrative expenses of 9,660 yuan, annual salary of the bureau director of 1,200 yuan, annual salary of the supervisor of 840 yuan. (Level 4) County education funds of 100,000 yuan or more, annual administrative expenses of 8,220 yuan, annual salary of the bureau director of 960 yuan, annual salary of the supervisor of 720 yuan. (Level 5) County education funds of less than 100,000 yuan, annual administrative expenses of 5,520 yuan, annual salary of the county bureau director of 720 yuan, annual salary of the supervisor of 540 yuan.

Ministry of Education Orders Tsinghua to Suspend the Law Department 108

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed Tsinghua University to actively expand the engineering college within its financial capacity and to temporarily suspend the enrollment of students in the law department starting from the next semester.

Former Director of Education Bureau of Pei County Under Custody 109

Ding Jianzhi, the former director of the Education Bureau of Pei County, has been out of office for a long time. More than 17,000 yuan of the cash that should be handed over during his term of office and more than 6,000 yuan of overspent and inflated accounts have not been handed over or accounted for. The county magistrate and the new director of the county have twice scheduled meetings to calculate and urge the handover, but he has repeatedly avoided and hidden for excuses. Yesterday, the Education Department received successive telegrams from the county magistrate and the director of the Education Bureau presenting the previous situation. At the same time, according to Zhu and others in the education sector of the county, Ding Jianzhi has been hiding in the City Hotel in the provincial capital, requesting that he be detained and escorted back to Pei County for liquidation in order to attach importance to education funds. The Education Department then sent personnel to investigate and found that the former director still had term deposits in Tongchangyi, Qin Yanshoutang, Yilong Company, and Xinpei Bookstore and other stores, totaling nearly 10,000 yuan, which he could not pay immediately. Therefore, the former director was temporarily taken into custody and handed over to Zhenjiang County for escort back to Pei County for liquidation, and the county magistrate of Pei County was ordered by the department to comply. Alumni Association of Graduates to Build a Clubhouse 110

The Alumni Association of Graduates of Nangaodongda Zhongda has spared no effort in developing its affairs since its establishment in the summer of the 19th year. In order to build a clubhouse, the association organized a fundraising team to raise funds separately. It is reported that more than 5,000 yuan has been raised. Situation After the Resumption of Classes at Taicang Middle School 111

Taicang Middle School, a provincial school in Jiangsu Province, was unable to start classes due to the Japanese invaders' repeated attempts to attack Taicang. The school authorities repeatedly gathered to discuss and seek other ways to relocate the school to hold classes. In mid-April, as the situation gradually became peaceful, it was decided to start classes at the original site on May 1. It is reported that since the school published notices and notified the students' families, half of the students have already registered. Classes have officially started on the 9th. It is recently reported that the school authorities, in view of the impact of the war on students' studies, have actively planned and formulated appropriate methods to intensify the curriculum in order to make up for the missed classes in March and April.

Xuyi County in northern Anhui Province has suffered from disasters and banditry in recent years, so that all the school fields are either in disaster areas or bandit dens. The sound of reading has not been interrupted. Now, the Education Association, Agricultural Association, various labor unions, various trade associations, various schools, and the County Party Department of the county all believe that Xu Zejun, the director of the Education Bureau, has been diligent and thrifty in his post for three years, benefiting the township and benefiting the youth.
